## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Validation] --> B{Check ID}
    B -->|ID is null| C[Raise ValidationError]
    B -->|ID invalid format| D[Raise ValidationError]
    B -->|ID valid UUID| E{Check container_type_id}
    E -->|Invalid UUID| F[Raise ValidationError]
    E -->|Valid UUID| G{Check Required Fields}
    G -->|Missing fields| H[Raise ValidationError with field list]
    G -->|All present| I[Validation Success]
    C --> J[End]
    D --> J
    F --> J
    H --> J
    I --> J
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Test as PatchContainerValidatorTest
    participant PC as PackageContainer
    participant Val as PackageContainerValidator
    participant Err as ValidationError
    Test->>PC: Create with id
    Test->>PC: Set container_type_id
    Test->>PC: Set tracking_number
    Test->>PC: Set original_unit_of_measurement
    Test->>PC: Set weight
    Test->>Val: validate(package_container, "PATCH")
    Val->>PC: Check id
    Val->>PC: Check container_type_id
    Val->>PC: Check required fields
    alt Validation Fails
        Val->>Err: Raise ValidationError
        Err-->>Test: Exception
    else Validation Succeeds
        Val-->>Test: Success
    end
```
